		focus = NEE_reintergrate_america
	}
	relative_position_id = NEE_send_the_redcoats_running
	x = -1
	y = 5
	
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	
	available = {
		has_government = paternal_autocrat

			tooltip = owns_all_american_states
			tag = NEE

			owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
			owns_state = 395 #Illinois
			owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
			owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
			NOT = {
				country_exists = TEX
				country_exists = CSA
				country_exists = USA
				country_exists = CAL
			}
			controls_all_owned_states = yes
		}
	}

		factor = 50
	}

			id = newengland.274
			days = 4
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			add_ideas = NEE_post_war_devestation
			add_ideas = NEE_republican_political_system
		}
	}
}

	focus = {
		id = NEE_american_imperialism
		icon = GFX_goal_HAI_civil_war
		cost = 5.00

			focus = NEE_back_in_business
		}
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = NEE_new_moralism
			focus = NEE_new_interventionism
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			is_in_faction = no
			OR = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
			has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		relative_position_id = NEE_back_in_business
		x = 7
		y = 1

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land
			}
		}

		available_if_capitulated = no
		cancel_if_invalid = yes

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus NEE_american_imperialism"
			create_faction = "league_of_american_states"
			add_ideas = USA_american_imperialism_idea
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.03 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.03 }
			add_stability = -0.05
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = isolation
				}
				add_ideas = civilian_economy
			}
